## ŌÜĪ EARLIER ŌĆö 2026-06-26 **PHASE H ┬Ę H5 increment 4 ŌĆö FORTIFICATIONS DEPTH COMPLETE (D142), closing the locked D138 UG:G-fidelity modern-engine push.** This is a **D74 gameplay carve-out**, not presentation-only: the modern engine now has staged entrenchments (**rifle pits / hasty cover ŌåÆ full parapet ŌåÆ redoubt / earthwork**), facing-aware works (front strongest, flank reduced, rear bypass still matters), stronger/clearer prepared abatis when tied to own parapets/redoubts, visible 2D/3D earthworks, HUD status, a player charge-impetus commit lock, and H5-i3's swamp/town/fort arrays now feed the universal T0 cover/move hooks (no per-battle fudge). **NEXT = H2 reenactment-footage decision or Phase I/J polish; Q5 Chattanooga + Q6 USCT battles remain LAST.**

Units that march off their own works lose the cover while the visible works fade. Abatis built by a brigade in its own parapet/redoubt is marked prepared, starts stronger, slows more, bites morale/disorder/fatigue harder, clears slower, and renders with clearer stakes/backing. 2D and 3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan fortification lesson.

AI inline charges stay unchanged. `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` now wires D141 terrain through `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor`: fort strong cover + attacker friction, town hard cover + street friction, swamp soft concealment + major slow, with the old wall/woods/hill ladder retained. This is ONE universal combat model; no scenario outcome gate.

## ŌÜĪ EARLIER ŌĆö 2026-06-26 **PHASE H ┬Ę H5 increment 3 ŌĆö TERRAIN READABILITY: the modern (non-hex) engine now makes high/low ground ŌĆö and EVERY topography type ŌĆö EXPLICIT (D141), the THIRD step of the locked D138 arc.** Three player-chosen **elevation modes** (default **HILLSHADE** relief = T21's, no double-count ┬Ę **CONTOURS** = iso-lines + elevation labels ┬Ę **COLOR-BY-HEIGHT** = a CVD-safe **Viridis** hypsometric tint), cycled from the in-battle settings drawer + the **R** key + the legend's mode chip; an **always-on compact LEGEND** (mode chip ┬Ę viridis gradient ┬Ę a live **on-hover elevation+type readout** ┬Ę a topography key of the types present); the 2D top-down finally shows relief it never had; and **swamp / town / fort** are now distinct render types. All PRESENTATION-ONLY ŌåÆ byte-identical. The hex engine IS Classic ŌĆö untouched.

> **ŌŁÉ THE i3 DISCIPLINE (read first ŌĆö the SAME as i2, NOT the i1 carve-out).** PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law. NEW `src/tactical/T22-terrain-readability.js` wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (fld3dInit / fld3dBuildTerrain / fld2dInit / fldPointerMove / fldExit; carries the ._wx/._atmo/._rr/._vf markers forward), reads-only, never writes sim/`fldRng`/`_SAVE_VER`. The elevation mode is a sim-UNREAD `G.settings.fldElevMode` (the renderRich pattern ŌĆö kept in `G.settings` only, NOT localStorage, so the documented "hillshade" DEFAULT holds every fresh session). The new **swamp/town/fort** terrain arrays (`__FIELD.terrain.swamps/towns/forts[]`) are **combat-INERT ŌĆö read by NO sim/combat function** (a probe static-scan enforces it), so combat stays byte-identical even though terrain was ADDED ŌåÆ proven `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff + `probe-bullrun` 15/15.
>
> **WHAT SHIPPED (D141) ŌĆö T22 (Ōēł630 lines) + thin T0/T6 seams.** (1) **3 modes**: HILLSHADE (3D = T21's slope-AO relief, T22 adds NOTHING to the 3D ground here so relief is never double-counted; 2D paints its own cached hillshade ŌĆö the top-down had none); CONTOURS (a 3D `LineSegments` of marching-squares iso-lines + elevation-label sprites; 2D = offscreen-cached polylines); COLOR-BY-HEIGHT (a 3D viridis-tinted overlay mesh; 2D = cached viridis canvas). The 3D hypso+contour are PREBUILT once and `.visible`-toggled per mode (snappy, no rebuild, no camera jerk). (2) **Legend + hover** ŌĆö `#fldElevLegend` (mode chip ┬Ę viridis gradient bar ┬Ę `#fldElevHover` live readout ┬Ę topography key). (3) **swamp/town/fort** distinct in 2D + 3D (swamp = wet-teal disc + reeds; town = clustered buildings; fort = angular earthwork berm + bastions); a demo set in the sandbox showcase. T0 seams: `fldBuildTerrain` gains the demo arrays; `fld2dDraw` calls the guarded `fldTrDrawGround2d` after the field fill; `fldKey` gains the `R` branch. T6: the drawer gains an "Elevation display" cycle control.
>
> **AARON'S 3 FORKS (AskUserQuestion):** palette = **Viridis** ┬Ę legend = **always-on compact panel** ┬Ę topography = **add swamp/town/fort** (visual-now / sim-cover-wiring-later ŌĆö that's what keeps i3 byte-identical).
>
> **BUG-HUNT (43 agents, 6 lenses ├Ś 3-skeptic refute + completeness critic):** 4 confirmed of 12 raw + 2 critic-new, **ALL FIXED before commit:** (perf) the 2D contour mode re-stroked ~600ŌĆō1600 segments EVERY frame ŌåÆ now rendered ONCE to an offscreen canvas (2 batched strokes) + blitted; (a11y MED) the legend mode/collapse buttons dropped keyboard focus to `<body>` on the innerHTML rebuild ŌåÆ focus restored in the click handlers; (MED) the legend topography key + height-range went STALE on a phase advance ŌåÆ a topography-aware legend signature now refreshes on any terrain change in BOTH renderers; (LOW) dropped the localStorage round-trip; (LOW) removed a redundant double-dispose of the cloned hypso mesh; (LOW) the per-pointer hover classify early-outs on a coarse cell; (robustness) the base-called 2D hook gained a full-body try/catch. > **The GM depth-chart's next rung is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬¦12.1 ŌĆö Army ŌåÆ Corps ŌåÆ **DIVISION** ŌåÆ Brigade), built on the Q10 corps chart (D108). A division can be staffed ONLY under a SEATED corps (the real chain of command), so the depth chart is a TREE built top-down. Teaches that a corps was only as good as its divisions ŌĆö A. P. Hill's "Light Division" and Hood's/Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions in Hancock's II Corps**.

>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (byte-identical until you seat a division; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership` ŌĆö an INPUT the bridge already reads ŌĆö via `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(╬Ż(`effDivRating`ŌłÆ64)├Ś0.03, ┬▒2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion) minus a `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his grade is below the **preferredGrade** ŌĆö a division was a **Maj. Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier where a CS corps was a Lt. Gen.'s), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads stretched until promoted. The lift is deliberately SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4) so the hierarchy holds: **army ┬▒17 > corps ┬▒4 > divisions ┬▒2.** No division seated ŌåÆ ╬Ż over zero slots ŌåÆ lift 0 ŌåÆ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf`. **ONE BILLET PER MAN** (army/corps/division mutually exclusive; seating-higher clears the division); **vacating a corps CASCADES** (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift ŌĆö enforced at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, cleaned on load-sanitize). `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:id}}` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered record on load. Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + capital (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).

## ŌÜĪ EARLIER ŌĆö 2026-06-23 **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART ŌĆö seat your generals into corps command over the Order-of-Battle tree; who you place (and whether his rank fits the billet) shapes how well the whole army fights** (overnight run, D108)

> **The GM depth-chart MOVE is shipped, built on the D106 OOB tree** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN ┬¦12.1/┬¦12.2/┬¦12.4 ŌĆö "an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), a new President's-Desk **"The Corps Command ŌĆö Depth Chart"** section lets the President SEAT pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (IŌĆōIV Corps), spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` ŌĆö the existing GM currency, no new resource). Each billet shows its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization ŌĆö Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps vs the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville.
>

It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership ŌåÆ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). ## ŌÜĪ EARLIER ŌĆö 2026-06-23 **Q8b: THE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE ŌĆö "scout the enemy" tier-reveals the enemy Order of Battle, scaled by your appointed general's cavalry** (overnight run, D107)

> **The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (┬¦15) is shipped, built on the D106 OOB board.** An **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the Command-desk Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` ŌĆö the existing GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. **Three tiers (┬¦15):** **light** (unscouted ŌĆö the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough count + the CTA) ŌåÆ **better** (scouted, cavalry < 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, no per-brigade detail) ŌåÆ **full** (scouted, cavalry Ōēź 65: the complete enemy OOB). With the 9 generals' cavalry, Grant (66) + Lee (70) ŌåÆ full, the rest ŌåÆ better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry. Intel is **fresh per engagement** (the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id ŌåÆ reverts to light when the battle changes). Teaches cavalry-as-the-army's-eyes ŌĆö Stuart's rides, and the Gettysburg intelligence vacuum when his cavalry was absent (a real Confederate command failure, not glorified).
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose scouting over the GM depth-chart MOVES (both unblocked by D106) because its scaling input (the `cavalry` persona attribute, spread 50ŌĆō70) + its `reveal` hook in `fldCampaignOOBHtml` BOTH already existed, `36-camp.js` explicitly deferred scouting to exactly this substrate, the D106 board already advertised a dead "Scout the enemy" CTA, and scouting is **pure display + an economy spend (never touches combat)** ŌĆö the safest byte-identity. The corps-billet MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks ŌĆö deferred next.

## ŌÜĪ EARLIER ŌĆö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q9 ŌĆö the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE: promote ┬Ę multi-currency ┬Ę merit gate)** (overnight run, D102)

Gen. ŌåÆ Maj. Gen. ŌåÆ Lt. Gen. ŌåÆ General**), spending a **multi-currency** budget ŌĆö **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary, shared with relief/appointment) **+ a NEW seniority pool** (`cmd.seniority`, accrues over the campaign, capped) ŌĆö and **merit-gated** by reputation. > **THE MERIT GATE (the honest history, the keystone):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep Ōēź bar) ŌåÆ a confidence bump (+3 rep); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) ŌåÆ a ├Ś1.8 capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation HIT (ŌłÆ4)**. Because OVR = 0.55┬Ęskill + 0.45┬Ęreputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** ŌĆö rank without merit doesn't make a good commander (teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence). Leapfrogging a passed-over senior adds a seniority surcharge.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path, no fudge):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small **BOUNDED** amount ŌĆö `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase grade-delta ├Ś 0.92), clamped to **Ōēż6** ŌĆö added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating ŌåÆ commandLeadership ŌåÆ` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). `cmdPromote` writes ONLY `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation` ŌĆö **never the scoreboard** (D74/D94 wall). **0 lift when un-promoted ŌåÆ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical** (live-sanity proven: a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79ŌåÆ80; the un-promoted skill reads identical with/without C for all 20 generals).

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q8 ŌĆö the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression)** (overnight run, D100)

> **The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign is shipped.** A new **"Camp" desk tab**: between battles the President DRILLS the army (4 foci ŌĆö musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance ŌĆö each toward a ceiling, costing fatigue; or **DELEGATE** to the field officer for a steady auto-sim gain) and reads the army's drill grade + the sitting general's OVR growth (PROGRESSION ŌĆö his reputation already evolves in `cmdOnResolve`). PURE INPUT-SEEDING (no scoreboard), and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp** ŌĆö proven, committed, pushed.
>
> **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; `C.president.camp` = drill{4 foci}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**) ┬Ę `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged) ┬Ę `campSetDelegate` ┬Ę **`campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM** ŌĆö per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled) ┬Ę `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue; a delegated army auto-drills; a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's SHARE erodes ŌĆö gated on `engaged`) ┬Ę `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`. **Drilling/progression only ŌĆö SCOUTING deferred to Q8b** (needs the strategic-next-battle Ōåö tactical-OOB mapping; logged).
>
> **The bridge seam (`src/85-battle-bridge.js`):** drilling lifts firepower (musketry) / morale (maneuver) / supply (entrenching) + relieves fatigue (endurance) + a small overall sharpness ŌĆö **bounded** (full-drill Ōēł +8 overall, Ōēż14; fatigue DRAGS it) ŌĆö EXACTLY 0 when undrilled ŌåÆ byte-identical. Wired: `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit), `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve), the "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js`, `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` + lazy-migrates via campInit ŌĆö no `_SAVE_VER` bump.
>
> **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop inert until the player opens the Camp (`campOnResolve` early-returns; `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill) ŌĆö a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build. NO RNG (deterministic).

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-4 ŌĆö the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" surge, inside the no-fudge wall)** (overnight run, D98)

> **The Madden layer now SWINGS a fight ŌĆö provably without ever touching the scoreboard.** An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and surges on ONE channel, hard-capped. Demonstrated: a single `foot_cavalry` badge on one CS sandbox brigade **flipped a deterministic US win into a CS win** (same seed), yet the total-casualty shift was only **17.2%** and the command aura peaked at **0.47 < the 0.9 wall** ŌĆö the rating reaches the result EMERGENTLY through bounded inputs, never by writing `cas`/`victory`/`men`/`sev`.
>
> **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), `_fldXFactorInZone` tests activation (march_vigor=moving ┬Ę his_offensive=moving/charging ┬Ę ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging ┬Ę last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) ┬Ę usct_assault/mass_assault=charging ┬Ę flanking=cav & charging). In the zone it surges **ONE channel = the declared lever**: a NON-speed X-Factor sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a SPEED X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT also surge the aura. One-shot ŌÜĪ `fldAnnounce`+`fldScenarioBanner` (`_xfOn` rising edge); `_xfGlow` marker pulse; deterministic `_fldXfDecay`ŌåÆ1 out of zone. **NO RNG.** A unit with no X-Factor is wholly untouched ŌåÆ byte-identical.
>
> **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` ŌĆö pushes the summed aura toward the **0.9 wall, never beyond**; strict no-op unless active. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (aura summed first), gated on `badges` (NOT officers) so both surge channels share one gate.
>
> **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` runs the surge + apply around `fldOfficersStep`; **`fldMoveFactor` clamps the COMBINED speed factor** (the `_spdMul` surge ├Ś the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** (exactly 1 ŌåÆ skipped ŌåÆ byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` ŌĆö a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font tofu), `reduceMotion`-honored. **Data:** added `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav) ŌåÆ 7 X-Factors; none assigned to a shipped roster yet (R-6) ŌåÆ byte-identical.
>

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö 2026-06-21 **CHICKAMAUGA ŌĆö the 3-phase Western epic shipped + adversarially hardened** (the woods ŌåÆ Longstreet's breakthrough ŌåÆ Thomas at Snodgrass Hill; probe 18/18) ŌĆö D90

> **Chickamauga is playable and verified ŌĆö the bloodiest battle of the Western theater, the fourth multi-phase epic, built on the T8 engine.** A new **ŌÜö BATTLE ŌĆö CHICKAMAUGA (1863)** main-menu button (rank 60, after Vicksburg) opens the side-choice card; command Bragg/Longstreet's army or Thomas's defense across three sectors in sequence: **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** ŌĆö a confused meeting engagement in blind timber; the Union line holds the road (historical). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20)** ŌĆö the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the moment Longstreet's column strikes the Brotherton farm; the CS pours through and routs the right (the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase). **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga** ŌĆö Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge until dusk, reinforced by Granger/Steedman, saving the army. Anti-Lost-Cause: **contingency over genius** (a staff blunder + a timing coincidence, not martial superiority) and **the squandered victory** (Bragg fails to pursue ŌåÆ the siege of Chattanooga ŌåÆ the November reversal).
>
> **Framing (decide-&-log, no fork):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" item = a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own milestone. **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** (the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive) ŌĆö the CS player is the offensive, the US player holds. This sets **Chattanooga up as the US-offensive MIRROR** (the next milestone; design brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`, which also banks the engine-grain lessons from this build). Universal gun model only; **no per-battle damage fudge** (D74).
>
> **Balance (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1); P2 **US-holds 32/32**, CS attacker pays **CS:US ~3.0** (the Fredericksburg failed-assault lesson); **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who closes the Wood gap in P1 **overturns** the battle (the alt-history hinge). The CS won the field yet **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) ŌĆö the costly-victory teaching, probe-guarded.
>
> **Research+verify (Workflow) corrected before authoring:** Hood Sep 20 / Maj. Gen. (not Sep 19 / Lt. Gen.); Helm under Breckinridge (not Cleburne); Cheatham restored; Granger & W.H.T. Walker = Maj. Gen.; Loring removed; gap-reporter flagged (Kellogg vs Bond); "River of Death" shipped only as disputed legend.

Gen."** (like Hans Heg; the BG dated to the battle but came after) ŌåÆ corrected to **Col. Harker** + a fact-check guard. ## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö 2026-06-21 **ENGINEERING CORPS ŌĆö increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING shipped + hardened ŌåÆ THE CORPS IS COMPLETE** (the pontoon train; player-only/byte-identical; probe 22/22) ŌĆö D89

> **The Tactical Engineering Corps is DONE ŌĆö all 3 of Aaron's locked "all of the above" (entrench + abatis + pontoons).** A NEW **opt-in river** (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) actually gates movement: a river is impassable except at a **crossing** ŌĆö a **shallow ford** (passable, slow + fatiguing), a **deep ford** (fordable only at Arcade; needs a bridge at Balanced/Historian), or a player-laid **pontoon bridge** (key **N** / "Pontoon" button): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time, opening a fast crossing. Surfaced via the **Skirmish ŌåÆ Ground ŌåÆ "River crossing"** option (+ an `opts.river` sandbox flag for the probe). The **B-5 realism slider** scales sapper speed, ford slow, AND fordable-vs-requires-pontoon; the strategic **Engineer Works Corps** (`bridgeArmy.engineering`) lays bridges faster on a campaign launch (the A1 anchor, via `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed`). 2D slate-water band + boat-deck pontoons + ford stepping-stones + labels (CVD-safe, reduceMotion-safe); 3D water plane + pontoon boats/deck; a citation-grade Fredericksburg/Rappahannock + James-River-1864 teaching card.
>
> **Architecture (byte-identical):** the active gate REUSES the two T0 seams reserved for it ŌĆö `fldEngMoveFactor` (ford slow) + `fldEngMoveGate` (returns a clamped bank point for an illegal water step). New T13 fns: `fldEngInstallRiver`, `fldEngCrossAt`, `_fldRiverNearest/_fldRiverBankPoint/_fldEngBridgeSite`, `fldSelPontoon`, the pontoon loop in `fldEngStep`, `fldEngDrawWater2d`, `fld3dBuildWater` + pontoon sync in `fld3dSyncEng`. **No shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon** ŌåÆ every AI-vs-AI baseline byte-for-byte unchanged (every read gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`; reset per-launch + per-phase). One T0 seam edit: `fldStepMovement` now settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD (the bug-hunt's soft-deadlock fix) ŌĆö `eg`-gated, so riverless baselines are identical.
>
> **DECISIONS (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** Bull Run's creek/Stone Bridge stay COSMETIC (making them live would regress a shipped, probed battle + break byte-identity); the active river is the opt-in feature, and the teaching card cites the Rappahannock as the historical anchor. AI river-pathing / AI-built works is the named T13 extension point (player-tool this increment, like D87/D88), so a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker forcing the crossing (river installed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank.
>
> **Bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus): 8 confirmed + 6 critic, all fixed.** HIGH: the gate's origin test let a unit on an open ford **sidestep into deep water and wade the band** ŌåÆ block entering blocked water from anywhere except already-blocked water + a midpoint sample (tangential bends). HIGH: the **3D water plane was buried under the opaque terrain** ŌåÆ raised to a thin on-ground sheet (+ fords lifted, no z-fight). HIGH: a unit ordered across impassable water **marched in place forever, fatigueŌåÆ100** ŌåÆ settle to HOLD at the bank. HIGH: the river skirmish was degenerate for a CS player ŌåÆ river placed by player side. MED: silent crossing refusal ŌåÆ aria-live halt announce + HUD line. LOW: dupe-span message; pontoon `side` + per-side cap.
>

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö 2026-06-18 Custom Battle Builder C4 complete Ō£ģ ŌĆö single-phase authoring, import/export, slots, launch gate green

> **Custom Battle Builder C4 is built and verified.** New `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow for player-authored real-time tactical scenarios. It covers scenario name/date/place, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, provenance, JSON import/export, shareable JSON, and six local persistence slots.
>
> **Architecture decision:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring remains deferred until a UI for `phases[]` can be proven as safe as authored historical phase data. Custom scenarios do **not** enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`; `fldScenarioData(id)` only falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` for explicit `custom_...` IDs. That preserves the exact historical battle roster while still launching valid custom scenarios through the same single-phase `fldScenarioInit` data path. Field size is reset every launch via `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H`, then a scenario may apply `field.w/h` safely.
>
> **Validation guardrails:** required metadata, safe unique IDs, malformed/unsafe JSON keys, duplicate IDs, bounds and numeric clamps, objective placement, reinforcement timing, side ownership, leader attach ownership, realistic artillery crew counts (12-40 per gun), forbidden combat/damage keys, and `phases[]` are all blocked. Custom artillery uses the universal `guns` model only; no per-custom-battle damage fudge was added.
>
> **Focused probe:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, universal gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**, with `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.json/png`.
>
> **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` ŌåÆ GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` ŌåÆ 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` ŌåÆ 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` ŌåÆ 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` ŌåÆ 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` ŌåÆ 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` ŌåÆ 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` ŌåÆ 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` ŌåÆ 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` ŌåÆ 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` ŌåÆ 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` ŌåÆ 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` ŌåÆ 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` ŌåÆ 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` ŌåÆ 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` ŌåÆ 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` ŌåÆ 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` ŌåÆ 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` ŌåÆ ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` ŌåÆ ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` ŌåÆ Classic paints, nonBlank 346; `git diff --check` ŌåÆ clean.

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1.5 ┬Ę THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL Ō£ģ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** ŌåÆ IMMEDIATE NEXT = ANTIETAM as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2)

> **The D74 "universal-combat" artillery cleanup ŌĆö the FIRST Antietam sub-milestone (do FIRST) ŌĆö is complete** (DECISIONS **D75**). Fredericksburg's per-battle **"volume-of-fire proxy men"** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) is REPLACED by a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Deliverable Ōēł**1749.6KB**.
>
> **Ō£ģ THE GUN MODEL (T5):** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL). `fldArtFireStr(u)` returns the fire-strength numerator (`fldResolveFire` divides by 1500): a battery with a GUN COUNT ŌåÆ `guns * 27 * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, crew-scaled so a battery fades smoothly as cannoneers fall); infantry / arms-off / a LEGACY no-`guns` battery ŌåÆ `u.men` EXACTLY as before. `guns` carried dataŌåÆunit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0) + `fldBrSpec` (T1); wired at `fldResolveFire`'s `strF`. CALIBRATED so a 6-gun battery ŌåÆ 162 Ōēł Bull Run's realistic 160-men/6-gun Griffin & Ricketts ŌåÆ the model REPRODUCES the existing batteries (consistent, not merely gated). The gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" (strategic strength flows through the Cannon-Corps `_canisterScale`, not raw volume ŌĆö documented).
>
> **Ō£ģ BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries); every baseline has none ŌåÆ `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` ŌåÆ byte-identical. **field 13 ┬Ę bullrun 15 ┬Ę fog 13 ┬Ę autopause 13 ┬Ę ai 15 ┬Ę campaign-link 16 ┬Ę officers 15 ┬Ę logistics 14 ┬Ę presets 26 ┬Ę csplayer 16 ┬Ę arms 23** ŌĆö all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.

The CS edge EMERGES from the wall's cover + the massed gun count + the cautious-attacker-dies-exposed geometry. ## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö run k (2026-06-16): **PHASE C-1 ┬Ę FREDERICKSBURG (Marye's Heights) Ō£ģ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** ŌåÆ NEXT = the next Eastern marquee battle (Antietam or Gettysburg, D69)

> **C-1 ŌĆö Fredericksburg, the SECOND data-driven tactical battle ŌĆö is complete** (DECISIONS **D73**). > **Ō£ģ C-1 ŌĆö the data-driven scenario spine + Fredericksburg:** `fldScenarioRegistry()`/`fldScenarioData(id)` (T1) map any id ŌåÆ `GAME_DATA.<battle>`; `fldScenarioInit` builds ANY registered id from the same shape (Bull Run byte-identical). The UI is generalized: `fldInjectScenarioButtons` iterates the registry (Bull Run keeps its bespoke marquee button; others build from `data.menu`) and returns the last button so the skirmish/preset buttons anchor after the block; `fldLaunchBattle` fires the briefing for ANY scenario; `fldScenarioSideChoice(id,go)` reads `sd.sides` (a per-battle side-choice card; `fldBullRunSideChoice` is now an alias); `fldBriefObjectiveHtml` keeps the keyword skeleton + a data flavor (`sd.brief`); `fldScenarioEndHtml` keeps the Bull Run branch byte-identical (shared `_fldScenarioEndBox`) + a data `sd.endNote` branch. `bullrun.json` gained inert `sides`/`brief`.
>
> **Ō£ģ THE DOOMED-FRONTAL-ASSAULT POSTURE (the headline mechanic ŌĆö a scenario-gated T0 seam):** the B-1 attacker AI is *competent* (fog-off it column-rushes + presses the mass bayonet), which Fredericksburg's assault was NOT. `data.assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` ŌåÆ `__FIELD._atkCautious` makes the AI attacker advance IN LINE across the open glacis and trade but never column-rush nor carry the wall (Burnside's piecemeal disaster). `var aggressive = !__FIELD.fog && !__FIELD._atkCautious` gates the assault/column branches ŌåÆ **default off ŌåÆ Bull Run/sandbox/skirmish/campaign BYTE-IDENTICAL.** A HUMAN Union player is unbound (the alt-history hook). Fredericksburg keeps **fog OFF** (the morning fog had LIFTED ŌĆö clear fields of fire) and wins the defense by the cautious posture + the stone wall (cover 1.7) + massed crest canister ŌĆö a DIFFERENT, battle-faithful lever from Bull Run's fog (no contradiction of "fog aids the defender").
>

## ŌÜĪ CONTINUE HERE ŌĆö run k (2026-06-15): **PHASE B-3 ┬Ę IN-BATTLE LOGISTICS Ō£ģ SHIPPED + VETTED + PUSHED** ŌåÆ NEXT = B-4 distinct arm roles

> **PHASE B-3 ŌĆö the ammunition economy on the real-time field ŌĆö is complete** (DECISIONS **D66**). New `src/tactical/T4-logistics.js` + guarded T0 seams + the Bull Run `supply` block + `tools/probe-logistics.mjs`. Deliverable Ōēł**1608KB**.
>
> **Ō£ģ B-3 ŌĆö supply trains + resupply + exhaustion:** each side fields a rear **ammunition train** with a finite **reserve**; a DISENGAGED brigade within reach refills (draining the reserve); a brigade OUT of cartridges holding the objective fires dry ŌåÆ bayonet (the 20th Maine); a SPENT brigade (fatigue>84) drags. The **attacker's train sits far behind its start line** (it outruns its supply) and the **defender's just behind the objective** ŌåÆ balance-neutral. **Ties strategic supply:** the reserve scales with `bridgeArmy().supply`; a raid-supply order cuts the enemy's. Gated + BYTE-IDENTICAL behind `__FIELD.logistics` (the 7 baselines + officers set sticky `_logisticsOff`).
>
> **THE FOG FIX (the headline ŌĆö a HIGH bug-hunt finding, surfaced to Aaron):** with **fog ON**, logistics first INVERTED "fog aids the defender" (D58/D64) ŌĆö Bull Run AI-vs-AI fog-ON **CS 8/8 ŌåÆ 0/8** (under fog the attacker cycled fresh brigades to its safe far-rear train and out-sustained the long fire-trade). Aaron's first pick (a defender's-depot rule) provably did nothing (the defender wasn't the ammo-constrained side); the fix that works (Aaron-approved) is **choking the ATTACKER's resupply under fog** (`ATK_FOG_RESUPPLY`=0 ŌĆö an attacker advancing blind can't run its trains forward). **Result: logistics is balance-NEUTRAL in BOTH fog states ŌĆö fog-OFF CS 5/8, fog-ON CS 8/8** (each = the no-logistics baseline; fog-aids-defender preserved). A FOG REGRESSION GUARD probe step locks it.
>
> **Ō£ģ FULLY VETTED:** adversarial bug-hunt **64 agents ŌåÆ 9 confirmed + 2 critic gaps, ALL ADDRESSED** (1 HIGH fog + 6 LOW probe-fidelity/correctness: probe boundary test, two-sided balance band, asymmetry + fog-reveal + supply-curve probe steps, reinforcement-only-side train). **probe-logistics 14/14, 0 pe** ┬Ę full no-regression GREEN (7 baselines byte-identical ┬Ę bootprobe ok ┬Ę t1probe 14/14 ┬Ę diag-classic 346) ┬Ę wcag clean (1 HUD-contrast fix). Committed + pushed.

## 1 ┬Ę THE PROJECT IN ONE PARAGRAPH
"The Civil War" is becoming **the definitive teaching wargame: Ultimate General: Gettysburg's combat FEEL + Paradox-grade strategic DEPTH + a museum's historical RIGOR** ŌĆö all three, no compromise. You are the **President (Lincoln or Davis)** running the entire war (economy, politics, diplomacy, morale, generals, the home front) AND commanding the battles in a real-time, gridless, drag-to-maneuver tactical engine ŌĆö wrapped in a PhD-level history + alternate-history teaching layer where scholarly consensus is the *favored-but-not-guaranteed* path. **The governing design law (Aaron's central tension, resolved): the simple low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun CORE that stands alone; ALL depth is optional ŌĆö auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able; education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real in-game mastery (so learning and fun pull the SAME direction).** One engine must serve the pure-battle player, the grand-strategist, and the PhD-historian simultaneously.

## 2 ┬Ę WHERE THINGS STAND (run h, verified)
- **Classic (hex, turn-based) is FROZEN/finished** ŌĆö the complete hex lineage + its 3D-skin "Modern." NEVER regress it (`tools/diag-classic.mjs` every splice).
- **Shipped + GPU-verified this run (all reusable):** procedural unit motion; **131 real PD-photo leader portraits** (`assets/portraits/`, license-gated, side-split for Anderson/Gregg) with a closure refactor + upgraded engraving fallback; a fuller period UI pass (drawn order-icons, engraved frames, brass portrait mat). Plus the inherited cinematic 3D foundation (PBR terrain, HDRI, ACES/bloom post-FX, weather, props, camera) and the adaptive period audio score.
- **The shipped "Modern" is only a 3D re-skin of the hex-turn engine** ŌĆö it does NOT play like UG:G. The real-time tactical engine + the grand-strategy owner-mode are **NOT built yet** ŌĆö that's the next work.
- **DESIGN: 63 decisions LOCKED** across a 35-round popup design session (Aaron). Fully captured in `GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md` (Parts IŌĆōIII). **No new-engine code written yet** ŌĆö the next chat builds from the spec.

## 3 ┬Ę THE DOCS (read in this order ŌĆö you have zero prior context)

## 4 ┬Ę ARCHITECTURE DECISION (run h ŌĆö important)
**Modularize via a zero-dependency build step.** The scope (50ŌĆō100k+ lines) outgrows the single 14k-line file. Author the new engine in **source modules**; a tiny **node concat script** assembles the one shippable `civil_war_generals.html` (keep the $0/portable/open-and-play deliverable + `play.command`). Set this up FIRST in S0. Classic + the existing engine stay intact through the transition (move them into the build later, carefully, or keep the current HTML as the base the build appends to). Gate the BUILT output (parse/hex/Classic-regression). This replaces the append-only-single-file splice model for new work ŌĆö but the gate discipline carries over.

## 5 ┬Ę BUILD ORDER & PHASES (Aaron: STRATEGIC-FIRST, confirmed twice)
**Phase group S (grand-strategy owner-mode) FIRST, then phase group P (real-time tactical).** Battles use the EXISTING engine via a clean bridge until the UG:G engine swaps in.
- **S0 ŌĆö scaffold:** set up the module/build system; expand the War Department (`G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}`) into the President's-desk shell (period war-room UI); strategic-turn loop; save. Layered scenario onboarding (start ~1861, limited toolset).
- **S1 ŌĆö economy** (full asymmetric model + finance/inflation/blockade).
- **S2 ŌĆö executive decisions + 3-layer morale + the 1864 election; the advisor/cabinet system** (the linchpin: auto-manage + recommend + TEACH, per-domain delegation).
- **S3 ŌĆö alt-history engine** (tiered divergence + hinge-points + emergent toggle + curated scenarios; deterministic-by-performance with consensus framing; the "your war vs history" tracker).
- **S4 ŌĆö education layer** (multi-voice debate cards + deep-dives + codex from HISTORICAL-DATA.md; ambient teaching; difficulty/realism sliders; play-style presets; full a11y).
- **S5 ŌĆö victory/defeat** (asymmetric paths incl. **negotiated peace for both sides**, military-only hard-loss) + all campaign scopes; wire existing battles through the bridge ŌåÆ **playable full owner-mode war.**
- **THEN P0ŌĆōP5** (`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`): the real-time UG:G tactical engine (First Bull Run vertical slice first), swapping in behind the bridge.
Each phase: gate + real-GPU self-verify (probes you READ) + Classic no-regression + left in a working, polished state (ship-quality iteratively).

## 6 ┬Ę THE BALANCE PRINCIPLE (design law ŌĆö apply to EVERY system)
The simple, low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun core that works on its own. Every deep system is optional ŌĆö auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able mid-campaign. Education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real mastery (learning is rewarded by winning, not a chore-score). Presets + sliders let each player set their own balance. **If a feature forces depth on a battle-first player, it's wrong; if it denies depth to a strategist/historian, it's wrong.** (Full statement: GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN ┬¦27.)

## 7 ┬Ę TOOLCHAIN, GATES, GOTCHAS (proven ŌĆö reuse)
- **Gates every change:** `.bak` ŌåÆ parse (`node --check` the built/extracted `<script>`) ŌåÆ invalid-hex grep `0x[0-9a-fA-F]*[g-z]` = 0 ŌåÆ collision-grep new fns = 0. With the new build step, gate the assembled output.
- **Real-GPU self-verify (READ the PNGs/probes):** `tools/shot-postfx.mjs`, `tools/shot-gpu.mjs`, `tools/shot-ui.mjs`, `tools/probe-motion.mjs`, `tools/probe-portraits.mjs`, `tools/bootprobe.mjs`, `tools/diag-classic.mjs`. Real GPU = **Intel UHD 617** via headed Chrome `--use-angle=metal`. A real-time sim/strategic loop needs an EMPIRICAL probe (sample state over frames), not just screenshots. Stale server: `lsof -ti tcp:8765 | xargs kill`.
- **Perf target:** smooth on the Intel UHD 617 at Auto tier; instancing/LOD/perf-tiers mandatory.
- **CRITICAL gotchas:** `G`/`HEX`/`PALETTE`/`THREE_BASE` are bare-name lexical globals (never `window.G`); THREE loads async (no top-level `new THREE.*`); override-by-redeclaration (last def wins); never a literal `*/` in a block comment; honor `reduceMotion` + `gfxQuality`; **NEVER regress Classic**; $0/free-CC0; Verified/Inferred provenance on all history.
- **Asset pipeline (historical run-H note; current top block supersedes live setup):** PD images via the run-h portrait pattern (Wikipedia REST summary ŌåÆ Commons license API PD-gate ŌåÆ download ŌåÆ `sips` resize). Extend to weapons/flags/USCT. Blender MCP remains available for future explicit 3D asset jobs (PolyHaven CC0 / Sketchfab), but Blender does not need to stay open unless a Phase-H asset task starts; free Hyper3D trial is drained.
